Peng Dehuai Captures Yuanzhou

Party and government agencies all burned down

Deng's brigade has recovered Yuan City

Peng's bandits scattered to Pingxiang and Lianhua

Nanchang Correspondence: The two bandit forces of Zhu Mao and Peng Huang, after the Gonghua incident, Zhu Mao led the pseudo First, Second, and Third Armies to disturb the border of Jiangxi and Guangdong from Nan'an and Xinfeng Dalou, while Peng Dehuai led the pseudo Fourth and Fifth Armies to ravage western Jiangxi and both banks of the Gan River from Ji'an to Zhangshu. It is found that Peng's bandits have about 5,000 people and more than 3,000 guns. Previously, because the attack on Jishui and Ji'an was unsuccessful, they besieged Anfu, Gao'an, Shanggao, and Fenyi counties. They were repelled by the Tang and Deng brigades and the police brigade. However, when Peng's bandits withdrew from Fenyi, they advanced towards Yuanzhou (i.e., Yichun) County from Binjiang in three routes. On the 23rd of last month, they had surrounded the county seat. At that time, there was only one company of soldiers in the city. County Magistrate Cai Shu, together with the company and the Jingwei Team, closed the city and defended it to the death. After 18 hours of fierce fighting, at about 4:00 pm on the 24th, the city was captured due to the exhaustion of ammunition and lack of reinforcements. The county magistrate disguised himself and escaped from the city to Fenyi. After the bandits entered the city, they burned down the county government, the Qingxiang Bureau, the Finance Bureau, the Party Headquarters, and the prison. All the prisoners were released, and the documents of the public groups were all burned. Shops of all sizes inside and outside the city were either extorted and then burned, robbed and then burned, burned if they did not pay, or burned because the people were not in the shop. All kinds of tragic situations are difficult to describe. After County Magistrate Cai escaped to Fenyi, he telegraphed Deng's brigade for assistance. Brigade Commander Deng ordered the Wang and Li regiments to lead more than 3,000 people to advance towards Yichun with County Magistrate Cai. On the 26th, they began to contact the bandits. After three days and nights of fierce fighting, Deng's brigade soldiers charged more than ten times, killing more than a thousand bandits before breaking through the main force of the bandits. Peng's bandits, unable to support themselves, collapsed and retreated out of the city through the south and west gates at 6:00 pm on the 28th, fleeing to Nanmiao, Zhongcun Lukou and other places under the county's jurisdiction. It is said that they turned to harass Lianhua, Pingxiang, and Wanzai counties. In Yichun city, ruined walls, broken tiles, and broken bodies were everywhere. The county government documents were completely destroyed. Yesterday, the provincial government and the headquarters of the 18th Division received telegrams from Regiment Commander Wang and County Magistrate Cai, reporting the above situation in detail.

After the General Command for Bandit Suppression in the province entered Ji'an on the 3rd, it has decided on the second step of the bandit suppression plan, and ordered the county magistrates of each county to state their opinions on bandit suppression for selection. In addition, Chairman Lu found that the county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs often fled at the first sign of bandit alarm, so that the communists were able to act recklessly. In addition to detaining the Wanzai County Magistrate and Public Security Bureau Chief who left their posts without authorization, he also telegraphed yesterday to the county magistrates of each county, urging them to be loyal to their duties, and to live or die with the city. (April 6th)

The Great Wind Disaster in the Provincial Capital of Guangdong

Dozens of people injured, killed, or drowned; the Jianghan warship sank

On the same day, ships traveling between Taishan and Xinchang were also sunk by the wind

Guangzhou Correspondence: In Ducheng, in the upper reaches of the West River in Guangdong Province, at about 6:00 am on the 30th of last month, a hurricane and hailstorm suddenly appeared, which had not been seen in a century, causing significant losses. That morning, a strong gale suddenly blew from the northwest, sweeping from the sea to the market, like ten thousand horses galloping, and dragons roaring and tigers howling. While residents were running for shelter, hailstones as large as chicken eggs suddenly fell from the sky, destroying about a dozen houses. The roof of a primary school in the city was also destroyed by the wind and hail. The Guangde Pawnshop was also blown down. Four men and women were crushed to death in the city, more than a dozen were seriously injured, and thirty were slightly injured. The anti-smoking inspection station on the riverbank completely collapsed, injuring five people. The disaster on the river was even more tragic. The Jianghan warship, which was anchored on the Ducheng river, was also sunk by the wind. It is found that the ship was one of the four major ships of the Jiangfang fleet. It departed to Wuzhou for combat a few days ago, and was recently ordered to return to the West River, cruising between Deqing and Ducheng to protect passing ships. Captain Pan Guoliu stayed in Wuzhou on official business, and only the deputy captain and dozens of officers and soldiers were on the ship. That morning, a strong wind suddenly rose, and the ship was directly hit. Because the west flow was turbulent, the ship's anchor was first broken. The ship lost support, the hurricane followed, and the ship sank into the river. Although all the officers and soldiers on the ship shouted for help, the ships had moved to other places to avoid the wind, and no one could rescue them. After a while, the ship sank into the water, and all the masts were not visible on the surface. Recently, the West River water level has risen six or seven feet higher than last month, and it will be difficult to tow the ship up in the future. On that day, the deputy captain and fifty or sixty officers and soldiers were mostly buried in the bellies of fish. About thirty people were rescued, which was also tragic. Because the wind and rain were urgent, the wires were also blown off. Therefore, the Fourth Fleet Command here only received the alarm the day after the ship sank. On the evening of the first, technicians and others were sent to the scene of the accident by the Suijiang warship. The Suijiang arrived on the morning of the second, and after the investigation was clear, personnel will be sent to find a way to recover the ship. It is heard that the Jianghan warship was invaluable, and the loss of the entire ship this time is no less than hundreds of thousands. On the morning of that day, in addition to the sinking of the Jianghan warship, hundreds of other civilian ships and small boats were blown to the river surface in Ducheng, half of which sank and half of which drifted with the waves. Fortunately, most of them were boatmen who could swim. It is estimated that about 300 men and women were rescued, and more than 20 young children drowned. The belongings on the boat have been washed away. The local party headquarters is now trying to accommodate the refugees. It is estimated that about 400 people are homeless, and the public hospital is temporarily used as a shelter. Also, on the Siyi side, the Xinhaishan steamboat, which travels between Taishan and Xinchangbu, was also sunk by a strong wind at Sanshe River on the same day. The ship had about 70 or 80 passengers. Except for 40 or 50 people rescued, it is estimated that 20 or 30 people drowned. Only twelve bodies were recovered the day before yesterday, and the rest have drifted away with the waves. (April 3rd)

Zhang Xueliang Appointed Commander-in-Chief of Aviation

Shenyang Correspondence: Zhang Xueliang, Commander of the Northeast Border Defense Army, concurrently served as Commander-in-Chief of the Aviation Army. At 12:00 noon today, the inauguration ceremony was held at the Dongta Aviation Office. Because the duties of the Commander-in-Chief were too heavy for him to handle concurrently, Zhang Huanxiang will be the acting Commander-in-Chief. The position of Deputy Commander will be promoted from the original captain Xu Shiying. Zhang arrived on time with Adjutant Tan Haihua. Fang Benren, representative of the National Government, and more than fifty important civil and military officials had arrived earlier. After the ceremony, Deputy Commander Xu Shiying read the oath of office on behalf of him. The words said, "We and our subordinates must abide by military discipline, absolutely obey orders, and do our best in our duties." After the reading, Zhang gave a public speech, saying that the Northeast Aviation Team has been reorganized into the Northeast Aviation Army today. Past experience has made us clear that the knowledge and training of the current aviation officers are not sufficient, so that it is nominal and regrettable. Now, in order to supplement the knowledge of all officers, it is decided to change the organization and increase a senior officer to supervise everything. Today's officers should step down to the status of students, and learn seriously. It must be known that the existing rank is not obtained by merit, and it should not be that because the rank is higher, they are unwilling to humble themselves to learn. From now on, we must break the line and work hard to learn, so that the Northeast Air Force is a useful air force that can apply science, and do not follow the mistakes of the former Chinese Navy. In the future, the acting Commander-in-Chief and Deputy Commander will strictly assess, and no favoritism will be allowed. Those who have achievements will be rewarded, and those who have no achievements will be punished. Those who destroy discipline and disregard the honor of the Northeast Aviation Army, even if they are executed by shooting, will not be spared." After the speech, all the people present went to the backyard to take pictures. Later, Zhang also introduced the acting Commander-in-Chief Zhang Huanxiang and Chief of Staff Chen Haihua to all the officers, and there was a very long speech. The main point was that by taking off the military uniform, they can be teachers and students to each other, and can be friends. There is no need to be polite when something happens. However, when wearing military uniforms, they should absolutely obey orders, otherwise they can be dealt with by military law. When speaking, his voice was stern. Finally, Zhang and all the people present walked to the airfield for inspection. There were 40 large and small aircraft. There were more than 100 aircraft that did not participate in the inspection. Zhang inspected for ten weeks and then took a car back home. (April 1st)

The Harbin International Association Newspaper Was Destroyed

The reason was for refusing to publish a reactionary declaration

Harbin Correspondence, 2nd: The Harbin International Association Newspaper was destroyed by the Communist Party at 11:00 am today, causing significant losses. All sectors of Harbin society are paying close attention. Newspaper offices and news agencies are especially concerned about the dangers faced by their peers. An emergency joint meeting was held at about 9:00 pm, and four items were resolved: (1) Representatives were immediately sent, one from each newspaper office, to the Governor's Office and various authorities to petition. If there is no proper solution within three days, all newspapers will suspend publication uniformly, and will not resume business until the problem is resolved. (2) The authorities were requested to arrest the culprits within three days and severely punish them. The authorities were asked to clarify who should be responsible for the damage to the International Association Newspaper, and other newspaper offices and news agencies should be effectively protected, and it should be guaranteed that such incidents will not happen again in the future. Newspaper offices and news agencies will be allowed to take armed self-defense if such incidents occur again in the future. (3) A telegram was sent to the whole country, requesting unified assistance. (4) In the future, no matter which newspaper office or news agency this happens to again, the industry will take unified action and help each other. After the meeting, the representatives who were elected went to the Special Zone Governor's Office, the Special Police Office, and the Daowai Public Security Bureau to see the authorities. Because it was already a banquet, Zhang Jinghui and Bao Wenjie were not there, and they left a petition and returned. That night, the major leaders of the Special Zone gathered at the Governor's Office for a meeting to discuss the aftermath of the International Association Newspaper case and the maintenance of local security. As a result, the Harbin Academy, which was not registered and had reactionary implications, was banned, and its students were disbanded. The management office ordered the arrest of the rioters who destroyed the International Association Newspaper, and they must be captured and interrogated overnight. Local security was tightened. Also, after 11:00 pm that night, more than a hundred people, similar to workers and students, gathered at the Harbin Academy in Qinjagang. The police detected this and sent a large team to surround and arrest more than ten people, all of whom were related to the destruction of the newspaper office. The president of the academy, Wang Xibai, and the director, Yu Ergui, escaped upon hearing the news and could not be captured. As for the details of the incident, on the evening of the 31st of last month, four Harbin Academy students, claiming to be representatives of the Harbin Freedom League, went to the International Association Newspaper and the Daowai Chenguang Newspaper, requesting to publish their declaration. Both newspapers refused to publish it because the content contained reactionary language. When the representative left, he said that if it was not published, the newspaper office would be destroyed and they would not be responsible. Both newspapers notified the police station that night, requesting protection. On the morning of the first, more than a hundred people, similar to workers and students, paraded in the streets, shouting reactionary slogans and distributing leaflets containing communist propaganda. Because the International Association Newspaper was heavily guarded, they crossed the street and went to the Chenguang Newspaper at 11:00 am. They shouted and cursed outside the door, wanting to enter and destroy it. Several representatives went upstairs to find the person in charge and questioned why they did not publish their declaration. Zhang Shuping, the editor-in-chief of the newspaper, came out to see them and told them that it was difficult for him to publish it. At that time, the rioters outside the door shouted and roared, and their momentum was fierce. Zhang repeatedly debated, and the rioters, seeing that there were more and more onlookers, did not dare to be too fierce, and posted a declaration outside the door and left. On the 2nd, the International Association Newspaper lifted the alert because the matter had passed. Unexpectedly, dozens of rioters gathered students in the style of ruffians from various schools early in the morning, first went to the Education Department of Qinjagang to petition, requesting permission for the Harbin Academy to register. The Education Department ignored them. The rioters waited for a long time without news, so they went to the International Association Newspaper, overturned seven racks of movable type in the factory, and trampled on them. A group of rioters went upstairs to search for the staff of the editorial department. Because the staff had not yet come to work, the rioters, seeing that there was nothing to do, destroyed the telephone and retreated. At that time, Zhang Fusheng, the president of the newspaper, rushed back to the newspaper office upon hearing the news, and notified the police on the one hand, and checked the losses on the other hand. Only seven racks of new lead type were worth about six or seven thousand yuan. The other scattered items that were destroyed could not be counted. The newspaper immediately sent a telegram to the Liaoning Border Defense Commander's Office, requesting that the Harbin authorities be ordered to deal with the aftermath, and telegraphed to major newspapers in the country, asking for their support. It is found that the Communist Party has been very active in Harbin recently, such as the Anti-Imperialist League, the League for Freedom, and other communist organizations, using false pretenses to create a great terror in Harbin within three months. The planned steps are to first surround public opinion and make it lose its authority, in order to be conducive to the records of their party. The authorities are ignorant, and they turn a blind eye to the rampant actions of the party, so that these people become more and more troublesome. The labor unrest and student unrest in Harbin have been happening one after another, and a crisis has been hidden in the society. When the Kaiming Bookstore was searched a few days ago, the party realized that the truth was gradually revealed, so it took a further clear action. It is heard that the behind-the-scenes manipulators of such incidents are Wang Xichen, the president of Harbin Academy, and Yu Ergui, the principal of the Eighth District Middle School and director of Harbin Academy, and several other people. After the incident happened today, both of them escaped. The Harbin Academy was ordered to be disbanded by the authorities.

Important News Two

The Bandits in Yangcheng Lake Have Been Repelled

Suzhou Correspondence: Zhang Ting, the second battalion commander of the Taihu Bandit Suppression Army, led his troops to suppress the lake bandits fiercely in the Sanzhuang area between Weiting Zhengyi on the 2nd of this month. He then transferred the 6th, 7th, and 8th companies to garrison Chefang. After the lake bandits were suppressed by Zhang's battalion, they fled to the Sanyuanchang of Chenji. The Chen Company of the first battalion of the 28th Bandit Suppression Army went to suppress them on the 4th, and the bandits collapsed and retreated. At 3:00 pm on the 6th, Battalion Commander Zhang, who was stationed in Chefang, reported that two large groups of lake bandits were found in Jiulinghu and Dayao Jinshan Temple near Chefang. Each group had more than 30 ships, and the total number of bandits was 800 to 900. One group sailed towards Jiulinghu, and the other group docked at Jinshan Temple. Battalion Commander Zhang, upon receiving the report, immediately led the Seventh Company and a platoon of machine guns, taking civilian boats and towing them with small wheels, to suppress them. They landed on the shore of Shenjiatang Village and charged towards the destination. At that time, most of the bandits were in Jinshan Temple. Seeing that officers and soldiers were coming to attack, they dispersed and opened fire to meet the enemy. The sound of guns and cannons was loud for a while. Battalion Commander Zhang commanded the troops, bravely charged, and fiercely suppressed them, killing more than ten bandits and capturing six bandit ships. There were two bandits in the ships. At that time, the bandits who did not have time to get off the ship fled to Songjiabang and other places. The forests there were dense, and the bandits used them to shield themselves from the target of the officers and soldiers. Later, a group of bandits from Jiulinghu also returned to Jinshan Temple to help resist the officers and soldiers. As a result, the bandit forces were strengthened, and they launched a fierce attack on the officers and soldiers. Fortunately, the officers and soldiers had occupied the high ground of Jinshan Temple and were able to defeat the many with the few. However, the bandits also resisted stubbornly, causing more than ten army soldiers to be injured. All of them were carried to Pan Shang with the help of villagers. Among them, there were a squad leader and a bugler, each of whom was seriously injured. The military and bandits fought fiercely until about 9:00 pm, when the bandits retreated into Cheng Lake one after another, and continued to fight against the officers and soldiers. The officers and soldiers were all on land and could not move forward. Returning fire to the bandits was not as powerful. Battalion Commander Zhang then ordered Staff Officer Liu to take the wounded soldiers back to Chefang by wheel. At first, it was planned to order the second platoon of the first squadron of the county police stationed there to go to the front line to assist, but because the police team guarded the key points, it was difficult to mobilize. Therefore, Staff Officer Liu transferred the fifth company of soldiers stationed in Xietang by telephone. After arriving at Chefang at about 10:00 pm, they transferred to the front line of Jinshan Temple to join the battle. At that time, a part of the bandits who had retreated into the lake landed again, so Battalion Commander Zhang commanded the troops to encircle and suppress them. At 1:00 am on the 7th, the bandits collapsed and retreated towards Cheng Lake. At the same time, the Bandit Suppression Command, according to the report from the military telephone, learned that the firepower of the officers and soldiers was insufficient after the bandits retreated into Cheng Lake, so it allocated two steel cannons, 6,000 rounds of rifle bullets, and 5,000 rounds of machine gun bullets that night at 12:00, and sent them by a police ship. In this battle, more than 40 bandits were killed and Zhang Pinhua, Lu Tongsheng, Gu Xinggen, and Xu Xiaodi were captured. On the army side, three people were killed and fourteen were injured. Nine of the seriously injured were sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, and the remaining five were sent to Gengsheng Hospital outside Qimen for treatment. Now Battalion Commander Zhang is still leading his troops to search and suppress them in the area. Gong Guoliang, the third district chief of the Suzhou Water Police, also led his team to Cheng Lake on the 7th to pursue and suppress the fleeing bandits. According to the villagers who came to the city from Dayao, the lake bandits who fired on the army in this battle were wearing miscellaneous uniforms. The firearms were long guns, box cannons, and pistols. Red cloth was tied on the wrists and gun handles as a mark, and there were also more than a dozen female bandits, all of whom were young and quite beautiful. By 1:00 am on the 7th, the bandits could not hold on and retreated east to Cheng Lake, but by about 6:00 am, faint gunshots could still be heard from Cheng Lake.

In addition, the Jiaozhi County Public Security Bureau also sent police to the Xuxu Temple today and found more than 20 pieces of luggage left by the bandits. Therefore, it is known that the bandits had spent the night in the Xuxu Temple beforehand. (Evening of the 7th)

Suzhou Continued News: The Seventh Company of the Second Battalion of the 25th Bandit Suppression Regiment opened fire with a large group of lake bandits in the Dayao area of Chefang Township the day before yesterday. It is said that the gang of lake bandits was a combination of the Haizhou and Siyang gangs. The bandit leader Zhang Zhaohua robbed Zhangyan Town in Jinshan County on the 1st of this month, and then fled back to Dianshan Lake to gather at Dayao. A meeting was held at the Jinshan Temple there. The stationed troops detected this and went to encircle and suppress them. They opened fire at 3:00 pm on the 6th, and the bandits began to collapse towards Yangcheng Lake at about 12:00 midnight. After investigation, in addition to more than 30 bandits being injured or killed, nine large and small hostages were rescued. All of them have been brought back to the General Command and their origins are being investigated one by one. (1) Zhang Yejin, ten years old, from Xinhang, Zhangyan. He was kidnapped from school on the 1st of this month. The bandits extorted 30,000 yuan, and his family has agreed to redeem him for 10,000 yuan. He was in the boat when the military and bandits opened fire, and his face was injured by stray bullets. There were also two young tickets, one named Zhu Pingjun, thirteen years old, from Zhangyan, and the other named Zhu Axi, thirteen years old, from Chenmu. (2) Zhang Chanquan, 25 years old, from Lili, a cashier at Qiaji Wheel Bureau Lili wheel. (3) Xu Aqiao, 16 years old, from Jiaozhi. (4) Xu Xiaodi, 17 years old, from Zhouxiang. (5) Gu Xingquan, 33 years old, from Meijiazhen. (6) Lu Tongsheng, 31 years old, from Zhouxiang. (7) Zhang Pinhua, 46 years old, from Meijiazhen. All of them are temporarily living in the command headquarters, waiting for notification to their families to come to Suzhou to claim them.

Today (the 8th) morning, the Second Battalion of the 25th Regiment also escorted a wounded ticket, Fei Yuxiang, to the Bandit Suppression Command. After being interrogated by the military court, he confessed that he was 20 years old, from Chajiatai, Beizha, Linghu, Wuxing, Zhejiang. He was kidnapped on February 12 while buying fish seedlings in Dongshan, Dingting. There were a total of twelve bandit ships at that time, and three tickets had already been kidnapped elsewhere. They were hidden in the boat together with Fei. The military judge sent Fei Yuxiang, who was seriously injured, to Huayan Hospital for treatment.

In addition, Gong Guoliang, the director of the Third District of the Water Police, led his teams, towed by the Peirong Zhenwei patrol ships and the Zhizhong speedboat, to Chenmu, Zhouzhuang, Jiaozhi, Xinta, Luxu and other places on the 2nd of this month, patrolling Yangcheng Lake and Dianshan Lake. At 3:00 pm on the 6th, the teams gathered at Shenjiabang, Fenghu, a few miles away from Luxu Town, and encountered more than 20 bandit ships led by the Shanghai gang Taibao A Shu (about 200 bandits). Seeing the officers and soldiers approaching, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest. Director Gong immediately ordered the troops to return fire. The two sides opened fire for about an hour, and the bandits fled in different directions towards Dianshan Lake after running out of ammunition. Three bandit ships were shot down, a young ticket was rescued, and five rifles were captured. Director Gong returned to Suzhou this morning. The Water Public Security Team under his command is still deployed in the Yangcheng Lake area. It is heard that the rescued ticket is named Zhou Quangen, 14 years old, from Wangjia Wharf, Nanshi, Shanghai. His father's name is Zhou Guisheng. There are eight people in the family, including his grandfather, brothers, and sisters. He went to Wanggangjing to burn incense on the 24th of last month. He was robbed by the Pudong gang bandits on the way through Dianshan Lake. At that time, three people were kidnapped together with Zhou Quangen. The names of the other two people are unknown. They are from Hongkou, Shanghai, one is 18 years old and the other is 14 years old. Their whereabouts are now unknown. After Director Gong returned to Suzhou, he prepared a document together with the ticket and sent them to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters for disposal. (8th)

Wuhu Quick News

The Wuhu Municipal Office has opened a pier donation. All business associations have requested a postponement of the levy due to the depression of commerce and the inability to bear additional burdens. If it is absolutely necessary, please reduce it to 2% of the Changguan tariff. The Municipal Office telegraphed the provincial government for instructions, and received a reply yesterday, only allowing it to be changed to 6%. After receiving the news, the General Chamber of Commerce still asked the Municipal Office to postpone the levy, otherwise they would unanimously strike and oppose it.

The new Director of Finance Sun Shengwu has not yet taken office because the provincial treasury revenue is extremely low after the division of national and provincial taxes in Anhui Province, and he feels financially difficult. He has now agreed with the Ministry of Finance to allocate 100,000 yuan per month from the national tax item for political expenses. It is heard that he will come to Anhui to take office within a few days.

The first Japanese hydroelectric warship, a destroyer of sixteen ships, arrived in Wuhu from Beijing at 8:00 am today. It is heard that it is scheduled to go to Wuhan this afternoon or tomorrow morning.

The contract period for Anhui egg tax has expired. The Finance Special Commissioner's Office invited merchants to bid for the contract. The bidding results were announced yesterday, and Deng Hanqiu won the bid to take over the business for 100,000 yuan. (6th)

Local Correspondence

松江

Jiang Erchang Arrested: Jiang Erchang, the former Executive Committee Member and Head of the Propaganda Department of this county, is currently engaged in quarrying stone from Tianma Mountain. On the 7th, the county government received a report from Zhang Fangqin, a resident of Tianma Mountain, stating that his uncle, Zhang Youshu, was coerced and taken away at gunpoint by Jiang Erchang's household, and is currently being held captive in Jiang's home, shackled with iron chains, only being released briefly during mealtimes. He requested the dispatch of a team for rescue, and claimed that Jiang's family possesses many firearms, etc. County Magistrate Jin immediately secretly ordered the second squad of the police team, leading ten armed officers, to go to the countryside at night accompanied by the reporter. They arrived in the town on the morning of the 8th, and together with Officer Chen from the Tianma Mountain branch station, went to arrest him at the address. Upon entering the house, they found Zhang Youshu's hands and feet bound by iron chains, which they immediately released. They began a search and discovered 1,545 assorted bullets, five assorted bayonets, one five-colored national flag, and a broken mahjong set. However, Jiang himself was not at home. They then detained his mother, Jiang Xie, and quarry workers Chen Wanzhang, Ma Yinghao, Xia Wansheng, and Yu Runtang, and escorted them onto a boat to return to Songjiang. The police team assigned five officers to watch the prisoners on the boat, while five officers proceeded on land to prevent accidents en route. As the boat was approaching the north of the town, they saw two people lying in ambush on the shore, armed and seemingly about to attack. The police team on land spotted them and moved forward to arrest them. The ambushers immediately fled and hid in a villager's home. The police team pursued them relentlessly and apprehended one of them. The other one escaped without a trace. The arrested person was identified by the reporter as being none other than Jiang Erchang, the main culprit who had kidnapped his uncle. He was also escorted onto the boat and taken to Songjiang to be handed over to the county. Officer Chen of the town later received a report from villager Tang Yisheng, stating that someone had fled into his house, leaving behind firearms and ammunition during the chase. He requested that they be retrieved. Officer Chen immediately went to Tang's house and found a rifle, five rows of bullets, a six-inch Browning pistol, thirty-three bullets (all loaded and not secured), a coat, and a rain hat. These were identified as the weapons and clothing discarded by Jiang Erchang after he fled into Tang's house. This has also been reported to the county by Officer Chen. The matter is currently under strict investigation. However, according to what Jiang told the police officers after his arrest, his younger sister was abducted by Zhang Youshu's nephew, who also took away many of her belongings. Therefore, he locked Youshu in his home, hoping that his abducted younger sister could be returned soon. He denied kidnapping for ransom. It is reported that the county's reorganization committee has telegraphed the provincial reorganization committee for instructions.

Qianjiawei Town Robbed by Bandits: Qianjiawei Town, belonging to Jinshan County, is only eighteen li away from Zhangyan Town. After the robbery in Zhangyan, rumors spread in the town, and merchants and residents were uneasy. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 6th, more than forty bandits arrived, all carrying rifles and pistols. They entered the town and looted fourteen shops, including Tang Shunchang, causing a total loss of approximately one thousand yuan. The Zhangyan Public Security Bureau chief, upon hearing the news, immediately sent a team to Qianjiawei to suppress the bandits. They exchanged fire, and the bandits fled towards the Xinjing area. It is rumored that this group also belongs to the "Taibao Ashu" gang. The Songjiang water police team has dispatched a ship to intercept them.

Recent News After the Zhangyan Robbery: After Zhangyan Town was robbed by lake bandits on the evening of the 1st, no relief efforts have been arranged. Furthermore, all the shops feel that their goods are incomplete and uneven, so they have not yet reopened. As of the 6th, among the men and women who were kidnapped, some have been released successively, but it is reported that there are still fourteen people who need to be ransomed. The bandits are demanding a huge sum of 100,000 yuan for Li Xinglin, the chairman of the chamber of commerce and manager of Yuanchang, but the Li family is not wealthy and cannot afford such a large sum. According to reports, on the day the bandits entered Zhangyan, the defense corps had received the news and were waiting. When they saw the first batch of three "Wushan" boats arriving, the defense corps fired machine guns. The three boats carried thirty-seven bandits, all skilled in shooting, who were assigned to be the vanguard. Unexpectedly, all were killed by machine guns. Subsequently, large numbers of bandits arrived continuously and went ashore to confront them, becoming increasingly numerous. The defense corps was unable to withstand them and retreated. Therefore, the bandit gang suffered considerable losses. According to the bandits and the released hostages, there are still eight bandit corpses that have not been found.

Qingpu

Lake Bandits Have Been Repelled by the Military and Police: Since lake bandits were discovered in various areas of the western countryside of this county, the situation has been tense, and rumors have arisen. After the military and police jointly suppressed them on three fronts, they have routed the lake bandits, who have retreated towards the Dian Lake area. However, the western countryside has many crisscrossing rivers and harbors, close to Dian Lake and Mao Lake. Although they are now distant, it is still difficult to completely eliminate them in the near future.

Young Woman Seduced and Flees with Lover: Cui, a resident of Fangjiawei Town in Qingpu County, is in his thirties and married to a woman named Zhang, who is twenty-four years old and somewhat attractive. She was seduced and bewitched by a police officer named Jia, stationed on the No. 5 boat in the town. On a certain day last month, she fled with him to Sijing Town in Songjiang County. By chance, Cui's cousin, Wang, spotted her in Sijing and secretly reported it to the public security bureau and defense corps of the town. The public security bureau and defense corps then dispatched police officers to pursue and arrest her. The seducing police officer took the opportunity to escape. Later, the woman was taken to the public security bureau, and Wang sent a letter to Cui. The next day, Cui went to the Sijing Public Security Bureau to take his wife back. The town chief, Chen Runchen, considered that the police officer's seduction and abduction of a woman from a good family was a matter of public morals, so he sent a letter to Captain Hao, requesting that the police officer be arrested and severely punished. Captain Hao, upon receiving the letter, was very angry and ordered his subordinates to arrest him. He also reported the whole incident to his superiors.

Wujiang

Hostages Kidnapped from Dragon King Temple Are All Safe: The Dragon King Temple, seven li away from the city, was robbed by bandits armed with weapons last month. The Jiahe and Ning'an steamboats were robbed, and more than sixty hostages were kidnapped. Forty or fifty people were released successively. The remaining hostages were ransomed separately. After repeated pleas, they were all released from Siducun, Taihu Lake, on the 2nd.

Luhu Detachment Stationed in Zhouzhuang: A bandit ship arrived in Luhu Town, belonging to the county, last month and extorted more than 3,000 yuan from the townspeople, causing panic. The day before yesterday, Commander Zhao specially stationed the entire third battalion and the first, second, and third companies of the first battalion in Luhu. The town's police force is now strong. Yesterday (the 6th), Commander Zhao sent the second and third companies of the first battalion to Zhouzhuang to deter them.

Wuxi

Please Exempt Slaughter Tax and Construction Special Levy: In the case of Wuxi's slaughter tax with a construction special levy, the county construction bureau received orders from the provincial department last year, urging them to collect it strictly. However, the meat merchants tried to reduce or exempt it, and the two sides insisted on their positions. Until the winter, the construction department finally approved to first collect half of the amount from December, donating five cents of silver for each slaughtered pig, with three months as a trial period. Now that the trial period has long expired, the construction department has repeatedly ordered the construction bureau to transfer the order to the slaughter tax contractor, Wang Yun'gong, to collect the full amount from March 1st. However, the meat merchants believe that last year's autumn harvest was poor, the market was bleak, and the fresh meat business was sluggish. After deliberation by the entire industry, they requested the construction department to cancel the construction special levy collected with the slaughter tax to alleviate business difficulties. The meat industry director, Jiang Hongzhang, has submitted the situation to the chamber of commerce, requesting it to forward the request on his behalf. The chamber of commerce submitted a request yesterday, asking the construction department to approve the cancellation of the original plan.

County Police Team Arrests Reactionary Suspects: Wuxi County Magistrate Sun Zuji has repeatedly received secret reports that reactionary elements are hiding in and around the city, plotting mischief. Shen Dagou, who was involved in the ax gang case secretly organized by Chen Nianzu, a standing committee member of the Shenxin Trade Union last year, has recently secretly returned to Wuxi and is secretly active. Reactionary slogans have been frequently found in the Badaitou area of the Shenxin factory outside the West Gate. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Sun immediately secretly ordered Zhu Zhenguo, the captain of the county police brigade, to go and arrest them. Captain Zhu, upon receiving the order, led special agents Wan Shen Rongting and others, disguised as workers, to Shenxin Factory No. 81 in the middle of the night the day before yesterday to carry out a search and arrest. They arrested Zhang San Da and Tang Xiangchen on the spot. Then they heard the roof tiles of No. 83 shaking, searched the roof, and arrested Shen Dagou, who was wanted by provincial order, and Chen A'qiao, another suspect, in the gap. They took Shen Dagou and the other three back to the brigade headquarters together. According to Shen Dagou's confession, he is 36 years old and from Yuqi. Last year, because of the Chen Nianzu case, he had served as the deputy standing committee member of the trade union. After Chen and others were arrested, he went to Caojiadu, Shanghai, to work as a handyman to make a living. He recently returned to Wuxi to seek business opportunities and was suddenly arrested. He firmly denied posting slogans. Zhang San Da confessed that he is 30 years old, from Qingcheng City, Nan Shuangmiao, and is currently a supervisor of the Shenxin Trade Union. He was very unwilling to do it and was forced to do so by the labor rectification committee. They did not hold secret meetings. Because the factory had a surplus of more than 900,000 last year, the workers should have received 6% according to regulations, but the factory only agreed to give 29,000 yuan. Because of this issue, they had been holding meetings to negotiate with the capitalists. He firmly denied being a member of the reorganization faction or possessing firearms. Tang Xiangchen confessed that he is 24 years old and from Wuxi. He did not ask about the posting of slogans by the reorganization faction. Zhang San Da is a very good person, so he was elected as a supervisor. Chen A'qiao confessed that he is 28 years old, from Dongtai. He usually works as a laborer, hauling manure, or pushing carts, and does not know anything about posting slogans. After receiving the confessions, Captain Zhu immediately prepared a document and sent them to the county, where Judge Zhou Chengshen conducted a trial. Because the case was related to reactionaries, he ordered them to be detained together pending investigation.

Strictly Prohibit Hoarding and Speculation: Wuxi County Government recently considered that rice prices are soaring, exceeding 16 yuan per stone, which is not only related to people's livelihood but also to local security. At the last meeting on food relief, in addition to deciding to purchase 1,000 tons of foreign rice to provide relief, they decided to strictly investigate and prohibit smuggling and hoarding. Yesterday, they issued a notice strictly prohibiting hoarding, speculation, and smuggling, and allowing people to report them. Once verified and caught, they will be severely punished. At the same time, they ordered the social investigation office to conduct a strict investigation and report every five days to ensure thoroughness.

Sodomy Case Occurs at Yihe Inn: Guo Ruiliang, a native of Jiangpoqiao Township, Jingyun City, belonging to the county, is a man who likes boys. Because he stayed at the Yihe Inn in Huangnibu, he had a homosexual relationship with Fei Yaoqing, a tea room attendant at the inn, and they were very close. Unexpectedly, his wife, Li, discovered the truth the day before yesterday and reported it to the police. They were both brought to the public security bureau, where Section Chief Qian Yaonian conducted a trial. According to Fei Li's confession, she had recently noticed that her husband's face was gaunt and, after much questioning, learned that her husband had been engaging in sodomy with Guo Ruiliang for two months. Fei Yaoqing confessed that he is 46 years old. Guo Ruiliang came to the inn on the sixteenth day of the first lunar month this year and stayed in the same bed with him, and they engaged in sodomy. Since then, Guo has come to bother him every two or three days and gave him two yuan per night. Guo Ruiliang confessed that he is 26 years old and used to work as a worker in the Hongda foundry in Shanghai. After staying at the inn, he had a sodomy affair with Fei Yaoqing and paid him two yuan for the room, etc. After receiving the confessions, Mr. Qian considered that Guo and Fei were both shameless and ordered them to be detained together. They were transferred to the county government for trial yesterday.

Changzhou

Patrol Leader Who Released Rice Boat Without Authorization Detained: The Erfen resident station of the Sifen Bureau of the Wuyi Public Security Bureau detained three rice boats heading abroad from Weicun. The county government was seeking instructions from the civil affairs department on how to handle the case. However, rice merchant Qian Fengtai and others, taking advantage of the fact that Patrol Officer Zhang Hanqin had come to the city, asked Zou Yubing, an assistant at the district office, to compel Guo Qinghai, the patrol leader guarding the rice boats, to release the boats. The Public Security Bureau, upon receiving the report, sent a team to the bureau on the 7th to escort Patrol Officer Guo. After a brief interrogation, he was transferred to the county court for trial. Patrol Officer Guo confessed the circumstances of being forced to release the boats. He was immediately ordered to be detained. As for Zou Yubing and others, the county government has ordered the Public Security Bureau to arrest and escort them for trial.

Citywide Blacksmith Strike: Blacksmiths throughout Wuyi City, due to soaring rice prices and difficult living conditions, jointly demanded that the shop owners increase their wages. They requested an increase of eight cents based on the original daily wage of two dimes and two cents, for a total daily wage of two dimes. The shop owners, due to poor business and lack of profits, were unable to agree. The blacksmiths immediately went on strike yesterday and will not stop until their demands are met. The shop owners then agreed to increase the wage by one or two cents. If they have to increase it to eight cents, they can only manage to cope. Therefore, this strike is not easy to resolve.

Zhenjiang

Court Executes Kidnappers by Firing Squad: Kidnappers Yu Chunhai, from Henan, and Zhang Deqing, from Anhui, along with fugitive Yang Genyuan and others, robbed Yang Huaide's house in Yanggang, Gaozi Township, of clothing and other items. They also kidnapped Yang's nine-year-old grandson and extorted a total of 1,520 yuan, which they divided and spent. In September last year, the two bandits again agreed to come to Zhenjiang to redeem cotton clothes. They were arrested by the detective team and sent to the local court's prosecutor's office for investigation and prosecution. After trial, they were sentenced to death. The case was submitted to the Jiangsu Higher Court and then to the provincial government for review. The provincial government, after deliberation, sent a secret letter to the court to carry out the original sentence. Therefore, at 2 p.m. yesterday, Prosecutor Xu identified the two criminals and escorted them to the new execution ground outside the North Gate to be executed by firing squad.

Head of Police Academy Replaced: Miao Bin, the head of the Jiangsu Provincial Police Academy, has been ordered to be removed from his post. The vacancy is currently filled by Wang Dashui, the head of the Ninth Branch Bureau of the Capital Police Department, who was appointed by Hu, the head of the Civil Affairs Department. Wang will come to the province to take the oath of office in the coming days.

Nantong

Military and Police Encircle and Suppress Local Bandits in the Eastern Countryside: Local bandits in the eastern countryside of Nantong are resisting government troops in towns such as Caopeng, Dongsheng, and Basuo. On the 7th, Liu's battalion of the Fifth Division joined forces with the provincial police team and encircled and suppressed them in four directions. The Civil Affairs Department dispatched the Junhe and Qianshui warships to block the supply of bandits in Huanben Port.

Two Police Team Leaders Dismissed and Arrested: Xu Guanhong, the captain of the county police squadron, was having a dissolute life with prostitutes in the eastern countryside. Wu Xuzhai, the squad leader, secretly went elsewhere, resulting in the entire team being surrounded and disarmed by bandits, losing seventy-seven rifles and a large number of bullets. Xu and Wu were dismissed and arrested by the county government. The court opened a trial on the 6th, recorded their confessions, and submitted them to the province for instructions on punishment. In addition, Yan Diannan, the captain of the county police brigade, was engaged in extortion, causing widespread resentment. The local community has jointly submitted a petition to the provincial government, requesting his swift removal.

Huzhou

Bandit Recruiting Soldiers for Army Arrested and Sent to County: The battalion headquarters of the 1st Battalion, 30th Regiment of the National Army stationed in Huzhou, arrested a bandit named Wei Guoan yesterday for recruiting soldiers. The battalion immediately prepared a document and sent him to the Wuxing County government for interrogation. According to his confession, he is 39 years old, a native of Dongyang, Zhejiang Province, and used to serve as a police officer in the 2nd Squad of the 11th Water Police Team stationed in Lincheng. Last month, he came to Huzhou to handle matters and is now helping at the recruiting office of the Central Hotel. After interrogation, he was immediately detained due to the matter of recruiting soldiers.

Jiashan

Defense Police Go to Countryside to Suppress Bandits: The County Public Security Bureau and the Chengxiang Defense Corps, having learned that bandits are hiding in villages near Yaozhuangqiao, jointly went to suppress them on the afternoon of the 6th to quell the bandit atmosphere.

How Cruel are the Kidnappers!: Qiu Siguan, who lives in Baihutou, a village seven miles east of Yuhui in this county, has a small but comfortable family and has been extorted by bandits several times. At about 8 p.m. yesterday, twenty-six or twenty-seven bandits with mixed accents, painted faces, red and green ribbons tied around their heads, carrying broadswords and pistols, rushed in. They immediately raped Qiu's daughter, Lin Bao, with many bandits taking turns, causing her severe injuries. She is now barely breathing. They then kidnapped Mr. and Mrs. Qiu. As they were leaving, some gamblers were returning and mistakenly thought that the police were coming to arrest them. The bandits fired shots, injuring Zhou Changxing in the left calf. Before leaving, they set fire to the house of the monk Lu and his dwelling.

Head of Autonomous Region Appointed: Zhu Jiahua, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, in order to complete the county organization of Zhejiang Province by the end of June as ordered, has recently, in addition to ordering the county government to comply with various lists, to deal with the implementation of the county organizations in turn and to report them at any time, has already appointed Li Bingcong, Lu Baozhi, Fu Jinkui, Zhang Xinggen and four others to be responsible for carrying out various matters in each autonomous region.

Hangzhou

Shipping Companies Discuss and Agree to Shoulder Reconstruction Donations: The Zhejiang Provincial Government has decided to collect a 10% reconstruction donation on all passenger and freight fares of ships, which is scheduled to take effect on April 1st. Previously, it was learned that only the Qianjiang and inland river shipping companies are currently implementing it, while the Shanghai-Ningbo lines are still negotiating the issue of guaranteeing the amount.

Six Sources of Funding for District Autonomy: The Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department stipulates six sources of funding for autonomous regions in various counties: (1) land tax, land price appreciation, and public land revenue; (2) inherent public funds and public property; (3) abandoned temple property; (4) revenue from district public enterprises; (5) usage fees, handling fees, and overdue fines; (6) subsidies or donations. As for how the county, district, and village councils will allocate and use the funds, it is said that it will depend on the size of the population, the amount of land tax, the strength of the financial resources, and the burden on the people.

Ningbo

Two Fire Accidents: The back house of the Yuanli rice store warehouse behind the Xiajia Bridge outside the south gate of Ningbo City suddenly caught fire at about 6 a.m. yesterday. It took more than an hour to put out the fire. It is estimated that one Yuanli rice store warehouse building, one Maosenji waterworks building, two Zhang Muji carving shop buildings, one Li Caiyuan family flat house, one Liang Dechang lantern shop flat house, and one Ruan Ahe family flat house were burned down, for a total loss of more than 3,000 yuan. Also, the Tongchun candle shop in Dongjiang Dongwuhe Bridge in Ningbo City accidentally caught fire at 2:30 a.m. today, burning down four buildings of the shop, with an estimated loss of more than 1,000 yuan. Fortunately, the shop was surrounded by walls, which prevented the fire from spreading to neighboring houses.

Large Number of Refugees Arrive at Qiyang Village Again: Qiyangchun in the southern countryside of Cixi was disturbed by Hubei refugees last month and was very alarmed. Unexpectedly, more than 300 Hunan refugees arrived yesterday. Fortunately, the police from the local public security bureau followed and monitored them, so there were no unexpected actions. Later, the village committee gave them money and rice, and they stayed overnight in the Tonglu Temple Qingmushan Temple and went to Shitan the next morning.

Letters to the Editor

Letter from Yang Shijie of Songjiang:

I was shocked to read the news about the divorce dispute in the Songjiang communication column of your newspaper's April 2nd foreign news. The details described in it are completely inconsistent with the facts. After I married Chen Yunyu, because of her violent nature, she often insulted my elders, and recently even pushed my mother down, causing her to be frightened, and left home for several days without returning, I filed a complaint with the Songjiang County Government requesting a divorce. Although it has been rejected by the Songjiang County First Instance, I am currently appealing. Therefore, my divorce from Ms. Chen Yunyu is entirely of my own volition and has nothing to do with my sister. Chen Yunyu has become even more unscrupulous after the verdict, gathering hooligans to harass my home. I am waiting for the legal solution and will not deal with her. The news said that I and my husband found my belongings, children's hats, etc. in my husband's sister's room, all of which are unfounded. As for the sections on secretly burning Yunyu's clothes and bedding, it is even more untrue. I am sending this letter to your editor and asking you to publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column as soon as possible to clarify the truth. With sincere regards, Yang Shijie, April 6th.

Letter from Yang Dinghou:

Dear Sir, I previously read in the local communications column of the third page of your newspaper on the 3rd of this month that Yang Dinghou, the director of the Qingpu Public Security Branch Bureau, was accused of being removed from his post. I checked that I was reappointed as the director of the Zhujiajiao Public Security Branch Bureau for the second time in May last year. Since taking office, it has been more than a year. Although I have not made any contributions to my job, I am fortunate that the local area is peaceful and I can barely fulfill my duties. However, recently, I have been suffering from minor ailments, resulting in a weak body, confused spirit, and difficult economic situation in the bureau, which is not enough to allocate, and it is very difficult to handle local affairs. Therefore, I specially applied for a long vacation to avoid mistakes in the future. Fortunately, I was approved by the Qingpu County Government and appointed Zhang Huaijin to take over. I handed over the matter clearly and reported it on the 3rd of this month. The report in your newspaper that the Civil Affairs Department removed Yang from his post is not in accordance with the facts and greatly hinders my reputation and future. Therefore, I am sending this letter to ask you to correct it immediately. With gratitude, Yang Dinghou, former director of the Qingpu County Public Security First Branch Bureau, April 6th.

Local News

Major Disturbance on Beijing Road Yesterday Morning

One Person Killed by Gunfire

Several People Detained

The Guomin News Agency reported that at 9:30 yesterday morning, forty to fifty workers and students were planning to hold a meeting at the Ningbo Fellow Association. Since the association had already taken precautions, the waiting patrolmen reported it to the police station by phone. The police station immediately dispatched five foreign patrolmen and sixteen Chinese patrolmen to disperse them and arrested three ringleaders. The crowd then moved to Beijing Road. At that time, the number had reached one hundred to two hundred people, planning to transfer from a certain candy store to a certain grand theater for a meeting. A shop assistant named Lin came out to stop them and was beaten. A Chinese patrolman standing there saw the beating and also saw people distributing communist leaflets. He immediately stepped forward to arrest one person. As he was preparing to take him to the police station, the crowd surged forward, resulting in a conflict with the Chinese patrolman. He immediately opened fire and killed one person. The remaining crowd dispersed. Later, a large number of patrolmen from the police station arrived and arrested four people on Guizhou Road and five people on Ningbo Road. After the incident, the Citizens Training Association, after conducting an investigation, wrote and issued a "Letter to Compatriots." The Third District Party Department also issued a "Letter to Comrades," detailing the causes of the incident.

It is also reported that the Freedom Grand Alliance has scheduled a general meeting of representatives from all walks of life to be held at the Ningbo Fellow Association on Tibet Road at 10 a.m. on the 10th of this month to discuss the case of Liu Yiqing's killing yesterday.

Yesterday's Taxpayers' Association Elected Group Representatives

Total of Fifty-Four People

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association held its election of commercial and fellow-provincial group representatives at 5:00 PM yesterday at the association's office at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. Geng Jiaji, representative of the Shanghai Municipal Government; Ye Hongji, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office; and representatives from various groups, including Chen Songyuan, Wang Yansong, Ye Fuxiao, Ni Jinlin, Lin Kanghou, Zou Quan, Li Bohan, Ren Xiangsheng, Zhang Yichen, Zou Juncheng, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Xiangzeng, Pan Xulun, and others, were present. Gao Wang Xiaolai, the chairman and Xu Jilun, the vice-chairman of the association, together with representatives from the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, formally opened the ballot boxes. An inspection of the votes revealed 80 ballots cast in the commercial group election and 35 in the fellow-provincial group election. Chen Songyuan, Zou Quan, Zhang Yichen, and Zhou Fuzhang were appointed as vote counters, and Hu Fengxiang and Sun Choucheng as vote announcers. The announced results of the election were as follows:

Turning Point for Chinese Steamers on the Yangtze

Since the summer of last year, Yangtze Chinese steamers have been suspended more often than sailing, resulting in direct and indirect business losses exceeding two million yuan. Recently, after repeated consultations between various shipping companies and the Transportation Department, the suspended steamers were gradually released. Furthermore, a portion of ocean-going vessels was reassigned to replace them, giving hope for the revival of Chinese shipping on the Yangtze River. This matter concerns the continuation and turning point of Chinese navigation on the Yangtze River, and a detailed investigation must be conducted, with the following points noted:

More Ships Resuming Operations: After the return of China Merchants' three major Yangtze steamers, the Jiang'an steamer also arrived in Shanghai yesterday, and the Jiangjing steamer will also return to Shanghai. Starting this week, classes 1, 4, 3, and 6 can operate as usual. However, the Kuaili, Jiangda, and Jiangtian steamers will be difficult to resume service for the time being. Nevertheless, with seven steamers available, this represents the highest number of ships resuming operations since April of last year. The Zhaoxing Company's Zhaoxing and Yuxing steamers, as well as the Ning Shao Company's Yongxing and Ning Shao steamers, have also fully resumed service. The Sanbei Company has first opened the Xin Ningxing and Minghe steamers, and the Changxing steamer, after repairs, will also soon be sailing. Each week, six to seven Chinese steamers are operating on the Yangtze River.

Emei Steamer Sailing on the Sichuan River: The recent strike by foreign steamers upstream presents the best opportunity for Chinese ships to compete in business. The Sanbei Company has reassigned the Changsha line's Hongyuan and Hongheng steamers to operate on the Yihan route. The China Merchants Bureau's Emei steamer, which was under repair in Shanghai, has reportedly been completed by the Jiangnan Shipyard and will undergo trial runs immediately. It is scheduled to travel to Hankou next week to operate on the Yichang line. If the decision on the Yingjiang and Erchao British and Japanese steamers remains unresolved, the Emei steamer will be instructed to operate on the Sichuan River to maintain navigational rights.

Contract for Egg Transport: The export volume of eggs from the Yangtze River is extremely large, with an annual value of over ten million yuan for shipments to Europe, America, and Japan. Traditionally, the majority of the transportation has been handled by Taikoo, Nisshin, and Jardine Matheson steamers. The annual shipping costs for eggs from Datong and Anqing alone amount to 130,000 taels. This year, Chinese shipping companies plan to reclaim the transportation rights for this cargo. Li Yunliang, the Business Section Chief of the China Merchants Bureau, personally went to Datong and other ports to negotiate with egg merchants. As a result, it was agreed that future shipments of Yangtze eggs to Shanghai would be exclusively transported by China Merchants and Sanbei Bureau steamers, with a shipping cost of 9.1 jiao per piece. It is reported that a contract has been signed.

Securing Cargo from Foreign Merchants: British and Japanese steamers on the Yangtze River typically handle the transshipment of goods from their respective countries, giving them a business advantage over Chinese steamers. Now that China Merchants, Sanbei, and others will soon have all their Yangtze steamers back in operation, relying solely on local cargo will limit their business. They must transship foreign goods to develop further. Therefore, Li Yunliang's trip to various ports along the Yangtze River for China Merchants Bureau was also to contact foreign merchants in Hankou and Yichang to negotiate the transshipment of foreign goods to Shanghai. This is currently underway in Hankou. In the future, there will be fierce competition between Chinese and foreign commercial steamers on the Yangtze River.

Changes to Insurance Procedures: Because of the potential for military involvement on the Yangtze River, the Shanghai Insurance Association has specifically agreed on two new regulations to notify all shipping bureaus: (1) If a ship is requisitioned or chartered by the government for military transport, the insurer must be notified. In addition to special fees, the original insurance policy will be suspended. If the requisition or charter lasts for more than ten days, the premium will be refunded on a daily basis. Failure to report will be considered a voluntary waiver. (2) These regulations will be implemented from the date of the resolution.

Chegouqiao Security Corps Disarmed by Bandits

At 7:30 PM on the 7th of this month, over 20 bandits suddenly arrived at the Wai Chegouqiao outpost of the Second District Security Corps of the county, surrounded it, and opened fire. The corps members were unable to resist and had three rifles and one Mauser pistol seized. Chen Zigui, Chief of the Third Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the alarm, immediately led over ten policemen to the Sunjiatang area, about half a li from Chegouqiao, and engaged the bandits. Both sides exchanged fire for several minutes, after which the bandits fled northeast. Coincidentally, security corps members from Guankou also heard the gunfire and arrived to join the pursuit. The bandits then crossed the river. At that time, a squad leader from the Chegouqiao Security Corps arrived in a state of disarray and, together with Chief Chen and others, inspected the outpost, finding two large pools of blood inside and outside the outpost. It was said that during the disarming, one bandit was wounded by gunfire and carried away by the other bandits.

Establishment of the Minhang Military, Police, and Corps Joint Defense Office

Due to the Major Robbery in Zhangyan

Minhang has 800 Troops

Since the major robbery in Zhangyan, Minhang, rumors have been rampant. To reassure the public, the First District Police Station in that area sent a letter to the First District of the Water Police Team, inviting the military, police, and corps units of the town to establish a joint defense office. The first meeting was held yesterday, attended by representatives from six organizations, including the First District Headquarters of the Water Police Team, the Detective Division of the Garrison Command, the Anti-Smuggling Camp, the First Public Security Bureau, and the First District Security Corps. Many important cases were discussed. However, due to strict confidentiality, the contents of the discussion are unknown. According to visitors from the town, there are currently over 800 troops stationed there, ensuring security.

Qi and Hai Counties Planning to Build Two Gunboats

To be Assigned to the Water Police for Bandit Suppression

Recently, piracy outside Wusong has become increasingly rampant, with coastal areas of Chongqi, Tonghai, and other counties being ravaged. Gentry and merchants from Qi and Hai counties, recognizing the weakness of the water police patrol boats in suppressing bandits, have jointly raised substantial funds to build two armored gunboats. These gunboats will be assigned to the Wusong Fourth District of the Provincial Public Security Water Police for management and deployment, strengthening their forces in hopes of thoroughly eliminating bandits, protecting the people, and safeguarding navigation. Yesterday, Gong Mianqin, the leader of the 17th Team stationed in Chongming, Fourth District, reported the situation to Zhu Bingzheng, the District Chief, who forwarded it to the Jiangsu Provincial Civil Affairs Department for approval and record.

Rice Prices Gradually Falling Slightly

The Rumor of Temporary Suspension of Trade in Zhabei is Absolutely False

Over 40,000 Shi of Rice Arriving in North and South Markets

According to Wuchen She, rice shipments have been abundant in the past two days, and market prices are gradually falling slightly. Some rice boats are still hoping for high prices to make large profits, while rice merchants and shops, seeing the market easing and supplies abundant, are mostly taking a wait-and-see approach. In addition, due to the abandoned lunar Qingming Festival and continuous rainy days, trading has been sluggish, and the market is in a state of stalemate. Yesterday, there were rumors that the Zhabei rice industry had temporarily suspended trading due to price restrictions by the Social Affairs Bureau, which is absolutely false. However, a few rice merchants are hoping for large profits and refusing to sell, resulting in limited trading. In the South Market, Su Tong Bai Geng rice continued to fall by one jiao, while foreign rice rose by one jiao. The cargo of Songjiang Bo Dao rice sold the day before yesterday has not yet been sold, due to weak buying interest. Over 80 rice boats, estimated at over 10,000 shi, are accumulated on the Pudong side. In the North Market, there are over 300 boats, estimated at 30,000+ shi of rice. If sales improve, it will be sufficient to meet demand.

Zheng Baozhao Succeeds

He has always had an exceptionally harmonious relationship with the employees. When the National Revolutionary Army arrived in Shanghai from Zhejiang in previous years, Mr. Yuan personally led the employees of the railway to work day and night, so the transportation at that time became smooth. It is understood that Mr. Yuan received an order from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, transferring him to the position of Director of Car Services on the Pinghan Railway. The vacancy will be filled by Zheng Baozhao, the former Car Service Inspector of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. Mr. Yuan is a native of Shangyu, Zhejiang. Great Boom in Shipping Chinese Cocoons to Japan

According to an investigation yesterday, due to the recent surge in the Sino-Japanese exchange rate, the shipping of Chinese export cocoons to various parts of Japan has been very crowded. Since January of this year, Chinese cocoon imports have exceeded 1,000 bales, which is an unprecedented phenomenon.

New Information on Chinese Silk Exports

Shipping Costs to Europe Soar: Since the rise of the "golden" expensive trend, all shipping costs have increased. Shipments to Europe have also increased covertly due to the use of shillings. However, the shipping cost of lake silk to the United Kingdom and France, which has always been calculated in taels, seems to be slightly lower compared to other goods. The British and French shipping companies in Shanghai have specifically consulted and revised the new shipping costs, specifically increasing the price of silk to Europe, rising from 1.6 to 2.5 taels per piece (weighing 112 pounds), which is unprecedented. The high shipping costs have truly broken all historical shipping rate records. From Shanghai to Marseille (France), London (England), Geneva, Naples (Italy), and Suez, the price of white silk per piece has increased from 17.8 taels to 19.45 taels, and the price of yellow silk per piece has increased from 13.8 taels to 20.5 taels. To Lyon, the price of white silk per piece has increased from 20.7 taels to 22.6 taels, and the price of yellow silk per piece has increased from 16.7 taels to 18.25 taels. To Paris, the price of white silk per piece has increased from 27.15 taels to 29.65 taels. To Moscow, the price of white silk per piece has increased from 27.6 taels to 30.15 taels, and the price of yellow silk per piece has increased from 23.6 taels to 25.75 taels. All other ports have also increased by more than 20% of the original amount. All customers have been notified.

Lake Silk Shipments to the United States are Crowded: Since May 1, the US Customs will increase import tariffs. After the telegram arrived in Shanghai, various foreign merchants in Shanghai rushed to ship their ordered goods to the United States in advance. The ships scheduled to arrive in the US before April 30 must carry as much as possible. Therefore, from last week until the Jefferson, Empress of Russia, and other ships exporting tomorrow, Shanghai has loaded over 4,000 bales of lake silk to the United States, worth about 5 million yuan. Other items such as beef leather, egg yolk, egg white, and tung oil are also being shipped in large quantities, so the congestion of shipments to the United States this week is truly exceptional, and all ships are fully loaded.
