Overview of Men's Volleyball

South China Has More Opportunities to Practice

Guangdong and Hong Kong Have a Good Chance in the Semifinals

The men's teams participating in the Volleyball Championship this year include Fujian, Tianjin, Zhejiang, Guangdong, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Hubei, Hong Kong, Liaoning, Shanghai, Hunan, Henan, Beiping, and Nanjing – a total of fourteen units. The women's teams include Guangdong, Jiangsu, Shanghai A, Liaoning, Anhui, Beiping A, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Tianjin, Hunan, Beiping B, Shanghai B, Yin, and Fujian – fourteen teams. Except for the Henan men's team and the Fujian women's team, which did not arrive due to reasons, there are actually thirteen teams competing for men and women, with a total of over 400 athletes. Talented individuals from the North and South gather together to learn from each other and improve through competition. This is an unprecedented event in the history of sports in our country. The spectators are extremely crowded during the matches, averaging around two to three thousand people. The scene is lively and prosperous. In the early stage of sports in our country, the enthusiasm for volleyball, which people are not normally interested in, is a good sign. The reporter has been on the scene every day, comparing the strengths of each team and understanding the situation of the competition over the past week. A simple overview is provided for those who are interested in this sport.

Volleyball in our country originated in South China. The climate in provinces like Fujian and Guangdong is warmer, making them suitable for this sport. As a result, more people practice it, the interest is stronger, and the technical progress is faster. Many talented individuals have emerged. The representatives of our country who have participated in the past Far Eastern Games have all been selected from these provinces, winning championships and bringing glory to the country. Therefore, historically speaking, the teams from Hong Kong, Guangdong, and Fujian are the best in this competition. However, the Shanghai team is also composed of the elite players from the city, making them one of the best in East China. Talented players like Cao Tingzan, Xie Baochang, and Li Xinbiao are all well-known. Unfortunately, they faced the strong Hong Kong team in the preliminary round and were defeated. Otherwise, they would have had a good chance of winning the second place. The Liaoning and Nanjing teams are relatively better. The talent in the two teams is average. However, Liaoning is located in the Northeast, where the weather is cold and there is more rain and snow. There are fewer opportunities for practice and a lack of competition with strong teams, so their experience is naturally worse. The Nanjing team is said to be represented by the Central Military Academy. Most of the team members are from Fujian and Guangdong and have a good foundation in this sport. However, they have not been formed for long, and it is difficult to say that their coordination is perfect. The strength in the match with Beiping wasn't weak. They have now won the next round and will compete against Hong Kong in the semifinals. The players from Jiangsu and Tianjin are also very skilled, but overall, they are not as balanced as Liaoning and Nanjing. As a result, they will face Guangdong in the next round, making it difficult for them to stand out. The other teams from Zhejiang, Hubei, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Beiping lack long-term practice and experience in battle. Their formation is scattered, their defense is negligent, and their coordination is not smooth. Therefore, they were eliminated in the preliminary round.

Volleyball has now entered the semifinal stage. Fujian vs. Guangdong and Hong Kong vs. Nanjing will soon compete against each other. From the reporter's perspective, Guangdong and Hong Kong have a better chance of winning. In terms of individual skills, Chen Xibing from the Hong Kong team is an exceptional talent. His smashing skills have reached perfection. No ball can escape his grasp. He is praised as the number one player in East Asia, and this is not an exaggeration.

Comments on Women's Volleyball

The Strength of Each Team Varies

But the Spirit Remains Consistent

Guangdong Team Has a Better Chance of Winning the Championship

Volleyball was introduced to our country relatively late. With the exception of the major commercial ports of Guangdong and Shanghai, very few people in the inland provinces practice it. Many don't even understand the rules well. It's even harder to popularize it among women. However, thirteen teams are competing in this tournament, which is unexpected. Although the strength of each team varies, their spirit remains consistent. The stronger teams are not arrogant because of their victories, and the weaker teams are not discouraged by their defeats. They truly understand the essence of sports, which is commendable.

The reason why the volleyball teams in South China are strong has been described in the previous section, and the same is true for women's teams. Based on the observation of the competition over the past seven days and the comparison of the results published daily, the Guangdong team has the highest chance of winning the championship. Shanghai A also has a good chance, but it will be more difficult for them to win against Guangdong. It depends on their luck at that time. The strength of Beiping A is also quite strong. Although they lost to Shanghai A, their excellent performance was praised by the audience. Therefore, people cannot be judged by their wins and losses. Shanghai B is an emerging force with a very lively style. If they can gain more experience through competition, there will be unlimited potential for their future development. The remaining teams are mostly located inland, with less exposure and slightly worse teaching methods. Therefore, they are flustered in battle, lacking coordination and unable to cope with strong opponents. This is due to the different environments they are in, and the talent of the players cannot be used as a standard. Now that Guangdong and Shanghai A have qualified for the finals, the competition on the 9th will be the key to the championship. The two teams will do their best to compete against each other. The performance at that time will surely meet the expectations of the audience.

Men's Basketball Championship

Entering a Close Combat Phase

Tianjin Will Easily Defeat Beiping

Shanghai to Compete with Hong Kong

Since the Shanghai team defeated Liaoning with a score of 53-44 and the Hong Kong team defeated Kobe with a score of 57-43 the day before, Hong Kong and Shanghai have each secured a place in the semifinals. It was originally scheduled for them to compete yesterday, but due to the unsuitable playing conditions of the two venues, the match was postponed to today. It is expected that there will be an extremely fierce competition. The other team that has qualified for the semifinals is Tianjin and Beiping. The two winning teams will then compete in the final to win the championship. Therefore, the men's basketball championship on these two days has entered a close combat phase. The past results and the current situation of each team are described in detail, so that the outcome of the championship can be predicted with a high degree of certainty.

Zhi Jiang University Swimming Pool, Photography: Lin Zeren

Past Results

Judging from the past results, in the first week of the first round, Tianjin first defeated Jiangxi with a score of 154-4. Jiangsu defeated Guangdong with a score of 40-27. Beiping won by default against Hunan. Zhejiang defeated Anhui with a score of 36-15. In the second week, Tianjin defeated Jiangsu with a score of 34-13. Beiping defeated Zhejiang with a score of 75-24. Therefore, the only remaining teams are Tianjin and Beiping. In the first week of the second round, Shanghai first won by default against Shandong. Liaoning defeated Fujian with a score of 89-16. Kobe defeated Hubei with a score of 91-46. Hong Kong defeated Nanjing with a score of 43-20. In the second week, Shanghai defeated Liaoning and Hong Kong defeated Kobe. The remaining teams are Hong Kong and Shanghai.

The Strength of the Four Teams

The four teams of Tianjin, Beiping, Shanghai, and Hong Kong each have their own strengths. Tianjin excels in cooperation and agility, Beiping has an advantage in physique, Shanghai is known for its accurate shooting, and Hong Kong is renowned for its liveliness and agility. Tianjin and Beiping have successively held the top position in North China. However, since the Beiping team was defeated by the Nankai team from Tianjin in the last North China Games, famous players such as Quan Yan have left the team, and the talent has declined. It is difficult for them to maintain their current state. The representatives of Beiping today are mostly new players. Although the newborn calves are not afraid of tigers, the five tigers of the Tianjin team are experienced and have the support of Yao Enhan from the Rotary Club, Li Qingan, the famous center from the YMCA, and the internal guard He Buyun. Therefore, it is predicted that Tianjin has a good chance of winning the match against Beiping.

Shanghai vs. Hong Kong

Next, let's talk about the match between Shanghai and Hong Kong. Although the Hong Kong team is lively and agile, the Shanghai team has a wealth of talent. Players such as He Rutong and Lu Zhongen are all famous players. The five-man zone defense is also well-practiced. It is predicted that Hong Kong will ultimately concede. But in any case, there will be a fierce battle. If Shanghai doesn't work hard, their future is uncertain.

Yesterday's Venue Rain Scene, Photography: Lin Zeren

Tianjin vs. Shanghai Finals

Based on general observations, the teams most likely to qualify for the finals are Tianjin and Shanghai. The strength of the two teams is evenly matched, and it is difficult to say who will win. However, Tianjin's cooperation skills and strategies seem to be slightly better than Shanghai's, based on past results. This is something that the Shanghai team should pay close attention to.

Brief Description of Women's Basketball

Shanghai, Beiping, and Guangdong Compete for the Championship

Hoping that Each Team Will Make a Final Effort

After the Shanghai team defeated the Jiangsu team by a large margin the day before, securing a place in the finals, their hopes for the championship have also increased. On the other hand, Guangdong and Beiping still need to compete against each other to compete for the final qualification. Judging from past results, Beiping seems to be slightly better than Guangdong. The Guangdong team is not very familiar with the rules of women's basketball, and they have been practicing again after arriving in Hangzhou, which is a disadvantage. The Beiping basketball team has long been famous in North China, and the forwards are particularly lively. If they meet Shanghai in the championship game in the future, there will be an unprecedented fierce battle. Chen Yingrui, the right forward of the Shanghai team, and Guo Xiaoping, the center, are particularly outstanding. Shanghai is likely to be the best in terms of shooting accuracy. However, in terms of physique, the Shanghai team seems to be inferior to Beiping and Guangdong. Therefore, it is difficult to say for sure who the champion will be at this time. In short, the teams with the best chances are Shanghai, Beiping, and Guangdong. It is hoped that the players of each team will make efforts to advance and those who put in the most effort will likely win the championship.

Men's Tennis Championship

Seizing the Overall Championship is a Key

Hong Kong and Shanghai Must Fight to the Death

Among the sports championships, the tennis championship is the most difficult to predict. This is because Lin Baohua from Shanghai, and Jiang Daozhang and He Jialiu from Hong Kong, have not been able to participate. Therefore, apart from the four teams from Guangdong, Shanghai, Beijing, and Hong Kong, which have stronger strength, the rest are average. After the elimination of the first and second rounds, only the four teams from Shanghai, Guangdong, Beijing, and Hong Kong remain, and they will meet in the semifinals.

In the afternoon of the day before yesterday, the four teams competed in the semifinals on the tennis court. Shanghai faced Guangdong, and Hong Kong faced Beijing. Each team played two singles matches. Zheng Zhaojia from Shanghai performed averagely, far less agile and lively than he was in Shanghai. Unfortunately, he was defeated. Wu Shaoxiang's performance has been very outstanding in recent days. The battle the day before yesterday was particularly remarkable. His opponent was Zhao Shilun from Guangdong, who tried his best to resist, but was ultimately defeated by Wu in both matches. As a result, Shanghai and Guangdong each won one match. Hong Kong defeated Nanjing in both matches without much effort. There is still one doubles match and two singles matches each. It was originally scheduled to continue the competition yesterday, but the weather was bad. There was heavy rain yesterday morning, and all the venues were very muddy and unusable. Therefore, it was changed to continue the competition today. Although it is impossible to determine who will win the final, Hong Kong's victory over Nanjing and qualification for the final is more certain than Shanghai's victory over Guangdong.

The outcome of this tennis championship is a key to the Hong Kong and Shanghai teams' quest for the overall championship. Apart from the all-around championship and the football championship that Shanghai can secure, they have no certainty in other events. Hong Kong can be confident in winning only in the swimming and baseball events. However, they also have a very good chance in volleyball. If the Shanghai team cannot win the tennis championship, then the overall championship will also be lost. Therefore, the Shanghai team must fight to the death for today's doubles match.

Who Will Win the Women's Tennis Championship? Shanghai and Tianjin Will Fight for It

Fourteen women's tennis teams have been fighting hard. The strong survive, the weak are eliminated. The winners stay, the losers go. The remaining teams are Tianjin and Guangdong, and Beiping and Shanghai. The results of the matches are that Tianjin won all two singles matches against Guangdong, and Shanghai won all two singles matches against Beiping. The outcome of the doubles match today will determine who will qualify for the final. Let's observe the past results to predict the future outcome.

Tianjin is More Likely to Win Against Guangdong

Tianjin was seeded in the preliminary round. Although they only won against Jiangsu in the second round, the Liang sisters have high tennis skills. Although Guangdong defeated Hubei and then defeated Nanjing, they cannot be underestimated. However, the results of the two battles were: (1) Liang Peiyao from Tianjin defeated Huang Yunyi from Guangdong with a score of 2-0, with scores of 6-4, 6-4. (2) Liang Peiyu from Tianjin defeated Deng Zhihao from Guangdong with a score of 2-0, with scores of 6-2, 6-4. In today's doubles match between the Liang sisters from Tianjin and Huang and Deng from Guangdong, Tianjin is likely to win. Although Guangdong still has Huang Nengqiu, it is feared that she will ultimately be unable to stem the tide. Therefore, Tianjin can win the first semifinal qualification.

Beiping Cannot Defeat Shanghai

The Beiping team first defeated Hunan, then defeated Liaoning, taking advantage of the momentum to meet Shanghai. However, Li Lian, the Javanese tennis flower of the Shanghai team, and Principal Kuai Shuping, a skilled female tennis player, are skilled in slicing, hitting, and pressing. Therefore, Li Lian defeated Du Lianjie from Beiping in the first match. In the second match, Liao Shuyun lost to Kuai Shuping. In today's doubles match, the Shanghai duo of Wang Dale and Su Zuqi will face Du and Liao from Tianjin. Shanghai's victory can be asserted. Even if they are defeated, the two singles matches will be switched, and Shanghai's victory will be easy.

Shanghai and Tianjin to Win the Championship in the End

The battle between Tianjin and Shanghai will determine who the champion will be. The strength of the two teams is evenly matched, and it is difficult to say who will win. The Liang sisters are not weak, and Li Lian and Kuai Shuping are also skilled players. Some say that Shanghai has a better chance, but the reporter dares not make a statement.

Football Musings

Championship Prediction

A total of twelve teams participated in this football competition. Due to the absence of the Beiping and Henan teams, only ten teams remain. In terms of strength, Shanghai is the strongest and can secure the championship. The next is the Guangdong team, followed by the Tianjin and Liaoning teams. Unexpectedly, the two teams failed in the second round and the semifinals, respectively. As a result, the Nanjing team jumped to second place. The Hong Kong team did not register for this competition, which is the most unfortunate thing. Otherwise, the situation of confrontation in the finals will be even more sensational and will add a lot of color to the conference.

Yesterday's Women's Dormitory Front Was a Sea of Water, Photography: Lin Zeren

In my personal opinion, the most pleasing in the past competitions are the passing skills of the Shanghai team and the running skills of the Guangdong team. The bravery of Tianjin and Liaoning, and the quirkiness of the Hunan team, are also enough to add color to the venue. In terms of individual skills, Chen Guangyao's dribbling, feinting east and attacking west, is as still as a virgin and as fast as a rabbit. Dai Linjing's hooked ball, heading, and turning around, and Chen Yutian's interception and turning, are as light as swallows, which can be said to have reached the stage. Zhou Xianyan's high blocks and diving saves have reached perfection and are truly rare talents in football. Other techniques, such as Li Ning's tackling and Chen Junpei's saves, have been recorded in the ball battle records and do not need to be described in detail.

Rah! Rah! Nonking!" drawing it out in an especially long cheer while the Liaoning team chanted "Good! Lao Liu, one more!" each cheer echoing and responding to the other. One side was soft and delicate, and the other was loud and strong. It was a beautiful story in the competition.

Spectators Lined Up Next to the Swimming Pool, Photography: Lin Zeren

The Significance of the Games

By Zhou Xiangxian, Deputy Director of the Games Organizing Committee

Since the Easternization of Europe, our country has been advocating sports for more than a day. However, it is a groundbreaking event for the Chinese nation when the government promotes athletes from various provinces to gather in one area, training constantly, competing again and again. The National Games, such as the one today, is a grand occasion. The various prizes prepared in the meeting are solemn and splendid, and listed in front of everyone. Those who are particularly strong won the championship, triumphant, and return. How dignified, how glorious. In sports, everyone has this psychology, that is, in the sports visit of you, also everyone has this concept, although, this only on the table to say.

Guangdong Swimming Athlete Chun Yuanhua, Photographer

Today's sports are based on the spirit of struggle, there is the physical education of the people, there is the heart of mutual encouragement and encouragement, and there is no intention of mutual jealousy and destruction. Victory is gratifying, and not winning is not enough to be humiliated. From the perspective of those who do not win, how can we know that this setback is not just to teach and perfect the other day's victory? Yue Wang Goujian's dwelling in Kuaiji, Napoleon's confinement in a deserted island, Columbus's anger at the boatmen, and finally finding the Americas were all victories from defeat. Moreover, the referees are fair and impartial, and come out to judge with the qualifications of obligations, without any selfishness. Even if the gap is a millimeter, it is inevitable to be uneven, all of which belong to compatriots, and will never be subject to the calculation of gains and losses, but will be ridiculed from outside. The views are so, I dare not remain silent, and I deeply hope that you will pay attention to the traces of sports, pay attention to the spirit of sports, and especially pay attention to the morality of sports.

Chief Jiang Visited the Meeting

Arriving in Hangzhou Today

Minister Jiang of the Ministry of Education is scheduled to arrive at the meeting today (9th) to attend the closing ceremony and deliver a speech. The senior officials of the National Government staying in Hangzhou will return to Nanjing after the end of the Games.

Stage Highlights

Splashing Waves: When the swimming competition was held the other day, the audience was packed, with hardly any space left. The pool was small, and with so many people swimming, the water moved a lot, causing waves to splash everywhere. Those who were close could see clearly, but the water splashed a lot.

Accumulated Water Forms Puddles: Yesterday's heavy rain caused the cancellation of the competition, and all the fields accumulated water. In some places, it was deep enough to submerge feet, especially on the track and field area. Looking out, it was a vast expanse of water. Workers were busy dredging and filling in depressions with mud. Even the command platform was damp and uncomfortable, a far cry from the grand scene of the previous few days. The unprecedented large dining hall, which could accommodate over two thousand people eating at the same time and seated 300 people, was originally covered with reed mats, which couldn't withstand the wind and rain. Yesterday morning's heavy rain, combined with the low-lying ground, turned it into a swamp in an instant. Thanks to the workers who rushed to dig small canals to drain the water, the situation was brought under control. Some athletes praised their efforts, saying they were no less than Yu the Great's taming of the floods.

Relieving Itch for Skills: Because the competition was postponed for a day, some athletes braved the rain to climb mountains, seek out secluded spots, and explore scenic areas. Others went boating on the lake to enjoy the unique charm of the lake in the rain, which was different from the lake under the clear sky. However, those who were less interested in boating and found it difficult to endure the itch for skills engaged in games of mahjong to pass the time. In the dining hall, on the tables where the ground was relatively high, male and female athletes were gathered, playing mahjong, poker, and other games of leisure without any monetary stakes. The joy was no less than that of intense matches.

Each According to Their Conscience: In the women's 200-meter relay race, the Eastern Special District team and the Guangdong team clashed, causing multiple disputes. After mediation, it was agreed to rerun the race. As a result, the Guangdong team did not show up, and the organizers were unable to cope. The representative of the Eastern Special District team made a long speech on the command platform, talking about relying on their conscience.

Finding Joy in Hardship: Reporters from various newspapers who were covering the news at the games all devoted themselves wholeheartedly to their work. Someone calculated that the reporters walked no less than 20,000 meters each day, which was as long as a race. Mr. Chen Shouyin, the business section chief of the Hangzhou Electric Power Plant, deeply understood the reporters' hardships. Yesterday, he specially distributed invitations saying, "You are responsible for guiding society and presiding over public opinion. This time, you are running around for the cause of sports, braving wind and dust, and working hard for the country. Our plant cordially invites you to a light meal at our cinema (referring to the Hangzhou Electric Power Plant's cinema) at 7 p.m. on the 8th of this month, and to watch a movie to soothe the loneliness of being away from home and to spend this precious moment. The beautiful scenery of the lake and mountains awaits you." The words were beautiful and sweet. The reporters, finding joy in hardship, were deeply grateful.

Rickshaw Drivers Get Northernized: In recent days, the rickshaw fares at the entrance of the venue have been very expensive. The rickshaw drivers are from the Jiangbei and Shaoxing gangs. Usually, they speak with heavy local accents, but these days, they can even speak Northern Mandarin, discussing fares in fluent Mandarin. They no longer say "a few jiaos (tenths of a yuan)," but instead say "a few maos (tenths of a yuan)." Yesterday morning, after the heavy rain, the shy sun gradually appeared in the afternoon. The general public knew that the final few days of the competition would mostly be championship finals, so many came to the venue. The city was emptied. When they arrived at the venue and learned of the postponement, they took the same rickshaws back, spending several yuan just to enjoy a ride. It was truly a waste.

Anxious Staff: Yesterday afternoon, Hangzhou cleared up, the clouds parted, and the sun came out, making it possible to continue the competition. Unfortunately, an urgent notice had been issued earlier, saying that "due to the continuous rain and the difficulty in using the fields, all competitions will be postponed by one day." Now that the rain had stopped, it would have been best not to affect the overall schedule. However, if they wanted to order the competitions to resume as scheduled, many athletes were out enjoying the lake and mountains and would be difficult to gather. The staff was anxiously rendered useless and merely became material for frivolous news. However, playful as the words were, they also offered a few earnest suggestions. Please tell the staff to be more careful in the future. If the announcement made yesterday morning had been a little more flexible, such as saying, "The competitions scheduled for the morning will be difficult to hold on time due to the rain. The competitions scheduled for the afternoon will be announced later depending on the weather," then there would have been no need to worry.

Free Talk

Rin Tin Tin Retires to His Hometown

— Sea Guest

Everyone who watches movies must know the dog star Rin Tin Tin. Rin Tin Tin is smart, chivalrous, and brave, practically surpassing humans. He was born in Alsace, France. He was first discovered by Captain Duncan, an American aviator. During the European War, when the United States joined the war, the captain was ordered to Europe to serve on the front lines. One day, he saw a puppy in a German trench. He loved its cleverness and immediately took it back to camp. After the war ended, he brought it back to the United States, and it became a movie star. He starred in many famous films at Warner Brothers, becoming colleagues with major stars like John Barrymore, Al Jolson, and others. His annual salary was about 25,000 pounds, equivalent to about 300,000 silver dollars. For a dog to achieve this, it is quite a feat. Rin Tin Tin is twelve years old this year, which is not considered old for a dog. However, according to recent news from Hollywood, he has retired. It's not because of physical weakness, nor is it because of the influence of sound movies. It's just that once during filming, for some reason, he could no longer be directed by his owner. No matter how the owner signaled to him, he wouldn't move. It shows that he has been overworked for years and has to retire from the film industry for a long period of rest. Fortunately, he has a lot of savings in the bank, so he can live a luxurious life in retirement. Soon, he may return to his hometown for a visit.

A Record of a Benevolent Thief Healing a Patient

— Tao An

Thieves are hated by the world. Who would have known that there could be someone who transcends the usual norms and conventions as described in this article? Readers might be surprised to think it's a record from overseas. The facts in the article are particularly interesting. Even thieves have principles, as evidenced here.

A certain gentleman in northern Anhui was working in a mine, diligently supervising the workers. One day, while walking around the factory, he accidentally tripped on a stone and bled excessively. He was bedridden and took leave to recuperate, but he did not recover after a long time. Coincidentally, there was a bandit alarm in the countryside, and the factory also suffered misfortune. The bandits were fierce and robbed as they pleased. When they reached his room, the gentleman suddenly got up and stopped them, saying, "Don't do this. I am a poor man. Apart from my sick body, I have nothing else. I am willing to offer my private savings of one hundred and several tens of yuan to you all. Please take it and don't frighten me. Otherwise, I will have no money for medical expenses later." The bandit leader thought for a moment and then generously returned some silver dollars, asking what ailment he suffered from. The gentleman pointed to his wound and explained the reason. The bandit said, "That's not difficult. I'll give you some good medicine." After speaking, he hurriedly left. The next morning, a person in green clothes arrived with a package of medicine. The instructions for treatment were very detailed. He tried applying it, and it worked. The gentleman once told people, "A loss may turn out to be a blessing. To get such good medicine in a remote village is truly good fortune in misfortune."

As the saying goes, "He who steals a hook is executed; he who steals a state becomes a prince." It is also said, "The great thief does not wield swords and spears," and "If the sage does not die, the great thief will not cease." There are many types of thieves. The one described by the gentleman probably belongs to a different category and cannot be compared to others. How can this not be recorded?

An Examination of Hens Turning into Roosters

— Xiu Jun

Reading Mr. Fei Gongzhi's article on hens turning into roosters, which is based on science and does not use superstitious language, is very enlightening. The article uses historical examples from the Han, Wei, and Jin dynasties to support its argument, citing them like family treasures. Although the original books are not listed in detail, the source of each reference is verified and based on historical records without any fabrication. This shows the importance of verifying facts, even for trivial matters, and the spirit of studying ancient texts. However, the article does not mention any cases after the Jin dynasty, which is a pity. I would like to add the following:

The "Book of Song, Treatise on the Five Elements" states: "In the twelfth year of the Yuanjia reign (435 AD), a hen in the Hualin Garden turned into a rooster." The "Old Book of Tang, Basic Annals of Empress Wu" states: "In the seventh month of the third year of the Chuigong reign (687 AD), a hen in Jizhou turned into a rooster. In the first month of the first year of the Yongchang reign (689 AD), a hen in Langzhou turned into a rooster. In August, a hen in Songzhou turned into a rooster." The "Jiangnan General Records" states: "In the second year of the Hongzhi reign (1489 AD), a hen in a commoner's house in Wuxian turned into a rooster." The "Ershen Yelu" states: "In the year of Jimao (the fourteenth year of the Zhengde reign, 1519 AD), a hen belonging to the Li Yan family in the western corner of Zhuji turned into a rooster, with a tail two or three feet long, like a brocade ribbon. The comb and feathers were all different." The "Yunnan General Records" states: "In the third year of the Jiajing reign (1524 AD), a hen belonging to the Zeng Ming family in Baoshan County turned into a rooster." The "Guizhou General Records" states: "In the fifteenth year of the Jiajing reign (1536 AD), a hen belonging to a commoner in Jinzhou turned into a rooster." The "Jiangnan General Records" states: "In the thirty-first year of the Jiajing reign (1552 AD), a hen in Jiading County turned into a rooster." The "Henan General Records" states: "In the thirty-ninth year of the Jiajing reign (1560 AD), a hen belonging to the student Qiao Weizhong turned into a rooster." The "Huguang General Records" states: "In the nineteenth year of the Wanli reign (1591 AD), a hen belonging to a commoner in Hengzhou Prefecture turned into a rooster." The "History of Ming, Treatise on the Five Elements" states: "In the sixth month of the twenty-second year of the Wanli reign (1594 AD), a hen belonging to a soldier's family in the Jingbian camp turned into a rooster. In the ninth year of the Chongzhen reign (1636 AD), a hen belonging to a commoner in Huai'an crowed and leaped, turning into a rooster."

In summary, I have included examples up to the late Ming dynasty. As for the Qing dynasty, there must be many such records as well. Unfortunately, the "History of Qing" is not yet completed, and I have few books at home, so I cannot verify them all. In short, when it comes to textual research, the collection of materials should be comprehensive and thorough. How can one impose arbitrary limits and leave out the victorious dynasty? If I have some free time in the future, I will add to it.

Peony Recipes

— Jun Mei

Peony Crisps: Magnolia flower petals are often used as a side dish in Suzhou restaurants. They are fragrant, crispy, and quite delicious. However, few people know that peony flowers can also be used as food. The method is to mix fresh peony petals with Xingping crisps and fry them in oil. Dip them in white sugar to eat. The taste is also exquisite and beautiful, not inferior to magnolia flower petals.

Peony Tea: Tea is for quenching thirst. However, bad tea leaves often make one more thirsty. Use peony petals to make tea. It is sweet, fragrant, cool, and thirst-quenching, and the color is bright and beautiful, making it especially enjoyable to appreciate. The petals must be picked the year before, pickled in sugar, and stored in a tin can for a year before they can be used. A guest gave me some, so I know about it.

What I Heard About the Bandit Situation

— Ren Peichu

Our Wujiang borders Taihu Lake and is often invaded by lake bandits. In the past, the bandits were weak and not a major problem. Since the Qi-Lu War, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway has been the site of battles for many years, and deserters have gathered in Taihu Lake. As a result, the bandits have become increasingly rampant. Last year, they even formed a group, calling themselves an army, and extorted and robbed various districts of Wujiang, leaving the people unable to sleep peacefully. Yesterday, I returned home and was told about the bandit situation by relatives and friends. Here are a few examples:

Negotiating for Military Expenses: Luxu is a small market town. At the end of last year, it was robbed by bandits, and many children and strong men were kidnapped. Those who were poor and unable to pay the ransom were all killed. The situation was very tragic. On the 30th of last month, the bandits came again. The residents were like frightened birds, quickly closing their doors and remaining silent. Surprisingly, this time the bandits were very polite and did not use any forceful means. After arriving, they negotiated with the police station to borrow 30,000 yuan to cover military expenses. They also produced a letter of appointment from a certain party, claiming to be a formal army. They promised to return the 30,000 yuan after receiving military expenses from the certain party in the future. After much negotiation, the matter was settled with 2,500 yuan.

Dr. Lin Has Great Luck: There is a Western-style doctor named Lin Zhiqin in Lili Town, who initially had no great reputation. At the beginning of last month, Dr. Lin took 500 yuan on a boat to Suzhou to buy medicine. On the way, they encountered bandits, and the entire boat was robbed. Dr. Lin was not spared. The bandits saw that he had a lot of money and asked him what he did for a living. Dr. Lin replied that he was a doctor. The bandits were pleased and immediately pulled him onto their boat and took him to their den, treating him very respectfully. They asked him to treat two bandits who were sick. Within three days, the bandits recovered. As a result, they treated him even more warmly and gave him 50 yuan as a gift. They let him return home. A few days later, the bandits came to Lili again and asked the police station for Dr. Lin's address. The police station said that there were several doctors named Lin in Lili and asked if they knew Dr. Lin's full name. They said no. At that time, another doctor, Mr. Ling Ganbo, was sipping tea in a tea shop. He heard that the bandits had arrived and were looking for Dr. Lin. Because Lin and Ling sound similar, he mistakenly thought they were going to kidnap him. He hurried home and fell on the way, causing his head to bleed. It was not until the bandit leader described Dr. Lin's appearance that they realized they were looking for Lin Zhiqin. Because Dr. Lin had already had one experience of entering the bandits' den, he was not afraid. He followed the bandits onto the boat and treated five bandits, earning 100 yuan in consultation fees. A few days later, the bandits recovered, and the bandit leader came to thank him. As a result, Dr. Lin's name became famous.

Red Carpet

A Record of the New York International House Welcoming Mei Lanfang

— Yang Linzhi

On March 2nd, 1920, I was traveling in New York, and the Chinese playwright Mei Lanfang was also traveling in America, being welcomed by Americans. That day, I met a Mr. Huang from Qingtian, Zhejiang, in New York. He told me that there would be a grand reception at the New York International House that evening to welcome Mei Lanfang. So I took the subway to go. I am writing a simple report to inform my fellow countrymen. I believe that readers will be happy to hear about it.

On the evening of March 2nd, Americans, admiring Mr. Mei's fame, specially held a welcoming party to see Mr. Mei's demeanor. The venue was borrowed from the New York International House, and the decoration was very exquisite. The security was also quite tight. The large number of people who attended showed the enthusiasm of the Americans for Mr. Mei. I drove there, and there was no space left in the venue. Besides the approximately one hundred Chinese people present, the rest were all Americans. If I had not been offered a seat by Mr. Pan Shao'e, I would have been afraid of wasting my trip. After waiting until the scheduled time for the welcoming party, Mr. Mei had not yet arrived. To relieve the boredom of the audience, the chairwoman, a certain lady, invited a certain Chinese lady to sing. The lady was dressed in Chinese clothes and was only ten years old. She was composed and sang a scene from "Mulian Saves His Mother," which was highly praised by the audience. The applause was deafening. Then, she sang a Fengyang folk song to thank the audience for their applause. However, Mr. Mei had still not arrived. Then, Mr. Xiong, the Consul General in New York, arrived. The chairwoman immediately invited him to speak. Mr. Xiong could not refuse and stood up to give a speech. He briefly said that Mr. Mei had specially come to your country for sightseeing. It is a great honor to have your compatriots hold a welcoming party. Mr. Mei originally planned to perform for two weeks and then return to China. Now, because of repeated requests from all walks of life, he has agreed to continue performing for a few days. The drama of our country is completely different from the drama of your country. But the audience was able to understand Mr. Mei's drama, which was completely unexpected. I found that the theater tickets are only sold for three dollars and eighty-five cents. But some people buy them and resell them for twelve dollars, and they are still not available. It can be said that the situation is extremely popular. Yesterday, when the news of the extension was released, the theater seats were already sold out. A friend asked me to book three seats for him, but I could not fulfill his request. I am very happy that the drama of our country is so warmly welcomed by your compatriots. Then, a certain American lady spoke about how the performance of Chinese opera was so orderly, which was rare. At this moment, Mei Lanfang arrived. The audience was like seeing clouds and rainbows after a long drought. The atmosphere in the entire venue changed. The chairwoman introduced Mr. Mei to the audience. Mr. Mei spoke in Chinese, which was translated by Mr. Zhang. He said that he was delayed because he did not know the way, so he was late. He apologized for making everyone wait. Today's venue is the International House, which is a place where international knowledge gathers. I came to America to seek knowledge and dare not say that I represent the art of our country. But I will offer my personal gains to your compatriots and hope for your guidance. Because I do not know the language, there are many barriers. I hope you will forgive me. After Mr. Mei finished speaking, the audience applauded greatly. Then, Mr. Zhang explained Chinese drama, such as "Holding the Whip as Riding." The meeting ended. It was already past ten o'clock. When the meeting was over, Mr. Mei had the difficulty of saying goodbye. Some of the audience shook hands with Mr. Mei, and others asked Mr. Mei to sign his name as a souvenir. When I left the meeting, Mr. Mei was still surrounded and could not escape. There is one more thing to tell the people of our country. The women who attended that evening were mostly dressed in Chinese clothes, which were bright and dazzling, not inferior to American clothes. I hope that our compatriots will pay attention to this.

Warmth in the Heart (166)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: Red Flames Soar, Hooked Balcony Admires Filial Daughter, Red Carpet Lies on the Ground, Instant Meeting with Famous Actors

When the day for the play came, the Qingliu Society sent Zuo Shichen several tickets and enclosed a letter, politely asking him to provide guidance on everything. Therefore, Zuo Shichen had arranged with Ruiyun in advance and explained it to the Grand Aunt, saying that he wanted to ask her to give Ruiyun a night off. If there were any hall songs to be sung, please send someone else to stand in. The Grand Aunt said, "It's a rare thing for your Second Young Master to invite her to see a play. Let her be happy for a day. For ordinary hall songs, I can ask Fengyun and Hanyun to stand in. But if the station ticket specifically states that she must go in person, it would be bad to offend the guests. In that case, we would have to ask for a stand-in. Anyway, just sit for a while and then come back to the theater." Ruiyun was unhappy when she heard this, saying, "Then I'd rather not go to the play. Hall songs coming in at one moment, Hall songs coming in at another moment. What's the point?" Zuo Shichen winked at her, saying, "Let them stand in. Anyway, we'll only ask for a stand-in if the station ticket specifically states that she must go in person." The play was scheduled to start at 7:30 that day, and the location wasn't far away. It was at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road, tucked away in an alley. People who had never been there wouldn't know that there was a theater inside. That day, Ruiyun didn't take her own carriage. She brought Ajin, and together with Zuo Shichen, they hired three rickshaws and went to the theater of the Moutrie Piano Company. As soon as they entered, they met the ushers of the Qingliu Society, who had a white rose pinned to their chest and a pink ribbon underneath, which read "Qingliu Society Usher." Zuo Shichen showed them the tickets in his hand. One of the ushers recognized him and said, "Are you Mr. Zuo? Please follow me." It turned out that although their theater was small, it was laid out like a foreign theater. The seats inside all had numbers. The numbers on the tickets matched the numbers on the seats. It wasn't like the old Chinese theaters, where people sat in a disorderly manner, grabbing seats. No matter what seat they grabbed, even if it was reserved for someone else, they would refuse to give it up. Even those who had reserved seats had no sense of order. In some theaters, they relied on a few ushers. If there were no familiar ushers, you wouldn't be able to get good seats. There were no ushers here. You just found your seat number according to your ticket, and there wouldn't be any confusion. Also, in the old theaters at that time, men and women sat separately, as if men and women sitting together would immediately lead to something scandalous, immediately giving them the opportunity to flirt. But in the main hall of the theater, men and women sat separately, while in the boxes, men and women didn't sit separately. If you asked the theater, they couldn't explain the reason. But in this theater, men and women sat together. At that time, it was considered very modern.
